# Formatting of some strings

STR_FORMAT_COMPANY_NUM                                          :(公司 {COMMA})
STR_FORMAT_GROUP_NAME                                           :组 {COMMA}
STR_FORMAT_INDUSTRY_NAME                                        :{TOWN} {STRING}
STR_FORMAT_WAYPOINT_NAME                                        :{TOWN} 路点
